                  You  may ask yourself - what the fuck is
                  this file supposed to be?  Well I do not
                  know  for  sure,  but  maybe  it's a new
                  ascii  collection  made  in hard work by
                  Paszczak  /cOR&aZK&vMF&oBS,  huh?   I am
                  creating  them  so  many,  lately...  ;)
                  (pienknie  sie  ubierasz  kochana)  It's
                  quite  crazy  to  release  above  25o kB
                  asciis during one week, ain't it?  Well,
                  I  think it's a bit crazy but you know -
                  aSCII rOOLES fOREVER!

                  So  I  hope  you  will like my styleez &
                  request some logos for your board, group
                  or   production.   (bardzo  myszka  lubi
                  kotka)  And  now enjoy this piece of art
                  created  for  you,  amiga scene!  And if
                  you  like my art give me a sign (message
                  or something) that you like it or not...
                  thanks!   (chodzi paszczak w kolo drogi,
                  czeka az sie zjawi stwor srogi...  ;)
